|A|=aᵢ₁Cᵢ₁+aᵢ₂Cᵢ₂+...+aᵢₙCᵢₙ ^8QK6HgDh

cofactor expansion ith row ^jqX0IEq8

|A|=a₁ᵢC₁ᵢ+a₂ᵢC₂ᵢ+...+aₙᵢCₙᵢ ^D4NQ5PVE

cofactor expansion ith column ^rPjftFdM

Tip: choose column/row w. most 0s  ^ge12G5NV

entire row/column of 0s ^S5R98Ebd

2 = rows/columns ^JqJz4zrX

 row/column multiple of another row/column ^HU0OzBHS

row operations on determinant ^CdKvkrZ4

if B = A w. a multiple of a row added to another one ⟶ det(A)=det(B) ^ndS4ct6d

if B = A w. 2 rows interchanged ⟶ -det(A)=det(B) ^EZ1zqtaz

if B = A w. 1 row multiplied by c⟶ c.det(A)=det(B) ^GpoZ6ILX

use to get ^JNzPDsRW

tip: create 0s in rows using these operations ^la9HB3g7

Examples ^7OnshGep

= concepts for columns ^vsQtMCPA
